                local function ni_(Gt,Al,zs,Ay,Sv)
                    local Vx,kk,Ka,Jg=Gt[Al],Gt[zs],Gt[Ay],Gt[Sv]

                    Jg=cl(su(_d(bh,3999-3983),Pq(bh,239168/14948)),92316027038730/21494);

                    kk=cl(su(_d(bh,-0.00050877639277537522*-23586),Pq(bh,-2923+2943)),4294971749-4454);

                    Jg=cl(su(_d(bh,1825+-1817),Pq(bh,-0.001211081394762073*-19817)),-116264764675650/-27070);
